191.	/test/bug463.jsp
	Due to limitations of the JSP standard, Makumba cannot make
a difference between the following two tags: 

<mak:object from="best.johnny.Season ssn" where="ssn.name = $season" >
^

<mak:object from="best.johnny.Season ssn" where="ssn.name = $season" >
^
To address this, add an id= attribute to one of the tags, and make sure that id is unique within the page.
